1:null
d:T18dd,<p>카카오 비즈메시지 관리 API (KAPI) — 카카오톡 채널의 알림톡 템플릿·발신프로필·이미지·그룹 등 발송 자원을 관리하는 API.</p>
<h3 id="연동-규격" data-spy-id="연동-규격" data-spy-section="공통-사항">연동 규격</h3>
<div class="md-tablewrap"><table><thead>
<tr>
<th>항목</th>
<th>값</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>프로토콜</td>
<td>HTTPS</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>도메인</td>
<td><code>https://kapi.ppurio.com/</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>메서드</td>
<td>POST 전용</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>인코딩</td>
<td>UTF-8</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Content-Type</td>
<td><code>application/json; charset=utf-8</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>인증</td>
<td>요청 본문 <code>bizId</code> + <code>apiKey</code> (Authorization 헤더 없음)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>권장 응답 대기 시간</td>
<td>15~40초</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></div><h3 id="인증-흐름" data-spy-id="인증-흐름" data-spy-section="공통-사항">인증 흐름</h3>
<p><svg viewBox="0 0 700 158" width="100%" style="max-width:700px;height:auto;font-family:inherit" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><defs><marker id="arc15" markerWidth="9" markerHeight="9" refX="8" refY="4.5" orient="auto"><path d="M0,0 L9,4.5 L0,9 z" fill="#2b3a4a"/></marker></defs><rect x="50" y="8" width="160" height="40" rx="6" fill="#bcd8ff" stroke="#2b3a4a" stroke-width="1.4"/><text x="130" y="32" font-size="12" font-weight="600" text-anchor="middle" fill="#1f2d3a">고객사</text><rect x="480" y="8" width="160" height="40" rx="6" fill="#f4f8fc" stroke="#2b3a4a" stroke-width="1.4"/><text x="560" y="26" font-size="11.5" font-weight="600" text-anchor="middle" fill="#1f2d3a">비즈뿌리오 서버</text><text x="560" y="41" font-size="9.5" text-anchor="middle" fill="#5a6b7a">(<a href="http://kapi.ppurio.com" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">kapi.ppurio.com</a>)</text><line x1="130" y1="48" x2="130" y2="148" stroke="#b8c6d2" stroke-width="1.2" stroke-dasharray="4 4"/><line x1="560" y1="48" x2="560" y2="148" stroke="#b8c6d2" stroke-width="1.2" stroke-dasharray="4 4"/><line x1="130" y1="80" x2="554" y2="80" stroke="#2b3a4a" stroke-width="1.5" marker-end="url(#arc15)"/><text x="342" y="72" font-size="10.5" text-anchor="middle" fill="#33424f">① 모든 API 요청 — 본문에 bizId + apiKey 포함</text><line x1="560" y1="116" x2="136" y2="116" stroke="#2b3a4a" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-dasharray="5 4" marker-end="url(#arc15)"/><text x="348" y="108" font-size="10.5" text-anchor="middle" fill="#33424f">② 결과 응답</text><text x="342" y="140" font-size="9.5" text-anchor="middle" fill="#5a6b7a"><tspan font-weight="700" fill="#1f2d3a">토큰 발급·Authorization 헤더 없음</tspan> — 매 요청마다 인증 정보 반복</text></svg></p>
<p>KAPI 는 별도 토큰 발급 절차가 없습니다. 매 요청마다 <code>bizId</code> 와 <code>apiKey</code> 를 본문에 포함합니다. 단, 발신프로필 등록을 위한 카카오 채널 인증 토큰 (Yellow ID 휴대폰 SMS 수신) 은 별도이며 <a href="/bizppurio-next-gh/kapi#프로필">프로필 API</a> 를 참고하세요.</p>
<h3 id="공통-응답-형식" data-spy-id="공통-응답-형식" data-spy-section="공통-사항">공통 응답 형식</h3>
<pre><code class="language-json">{ &quot;code&quot;: &quot;200&quot;, &quot;message&quot;: &quot;...&quot;, &quot;data&quot;: { ... } }
</code></pre>
<div class="md-tablewrap"><table><thead>
<tr>
<th>필드</th>
<th>설명</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>code</code></td>
<td>결과 코드 (<code>200</code> = 성공, 그 외 <a href="/bizppurio-next-gh/response-codes">코드 정의</a> 참고)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>message</code></td>
<td>결과 메시지</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>data</code></td>
<td>성공 시 응답 본문 (엔드포인트별 상이)</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></div><h3 id="rate-limit" data-spy-id="rate-limit" data-spy-section="공통-사항">Rate Limit</h3>
<ul>
<li>본 API 자체에 별도 명시된 Rate Limit 은 없으나, 비정상 다회 호출 시 일시 차단될 수 있습니다.</li>
<li>발송 자체는 비즈뿌리오 본 계정의 <a href="/bizppurio-next-gh/bizapi#공통-사항">메시지 API Rate Limit</a> 을 적용받습니다.</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="자원-↔-발송-연결" data-spy-id="자원-↔-발송-연결" data-spy-section="공통-사항">자원 ↔ 발송 연결</h3>
<p>KAPI 는 발송을 수행하지 않습니다. 발송은 <a href="/bizppurio-next-gh/bizapi#post-v3message"><code>POST /v3/message</code></a> (메시지 API) 또는 BIZCLIENT 의 <code>biz_msg</code> 테이블 INSERT 로 수행하며, KAPI 로 등록·관리한 자원이 발송 페이로드에 사용됩니다.</p>
<div class="md-tablewrap"><table><thead>
<tr>
<th>KAPI 에서 등록·관리</th>
<th>카카오 발송에서 사용</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>알림톡 템플릿 (<code>templateCode</code>)</td>
<td><code>content.at.templatecode</code> / <code>content.ai.templatecode</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>발신프로필 키 (<code>senderKey</code>)</td>
<td><code>content.at.senderkey</code> / <code>content.ai.senderkey</code> / <code>content.ut.senderkey</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>브랜드 메시지 템플릿 (<code>templateCode</code>)</td>
<td><code>content.ut.templatecode</code> (카카오 브랜드)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>이미지 키 (<code>imageId</code> / <code>imageUrl</code>)</td>
<td>발송 페이로드 내 이미지 URL/key</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>그룹 태그 키 (<code>groupTagKey</code>)</td>
<td>통계 분류 키</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></div><h3 id="추가-사항" data-spy-id="추가-사항" data-spy-section="공통-사항">추가 사항</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>템플릿 상태 변화</strong>
<ul>
<li><code>serviceStatus</code>: <code>REG</code> → <code>REQ</code> → <code>REJ</code> | <code>STP</code> | <code>RDY</code> → <code>ACT</code> → <code>DMT</code>/<code>BLK</code></li>
<li><code>status</code>: <code>S</code> (중지) / <code>A</code> (정상) / <code>R</code> (대기)</li>
<li><code>inspectionStatus</code>: <code>REG</code> → <code>REQ</code> → <code>REJ</code> | <code>APR</code> (승인)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>발신 프로필 키 타입</strong> (<code>senderKeyType</code>): <code>S</code> 일반 발신프로필 (기본값) / <code>G</code> 발신프로필 그룹</li>
</ul>

}1e:T5fb,<p>브랜드 메시지 기본형 템플릿을 등록합니다.
사전에 발신프로필이 등록되어 있어야 하고, 메시지 타입(<code>chatBubbleType</code>)에 맞는 이미지 규격을 사용해야 합니다.</p>
<h3>메시지 타입별 필수 파라미터</h3>
<div class="md-tablewrap"><table><thead>
<tr>
<th><code>chatBubbleType</code></th>
<th>필수</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>TEXT</code></td>
<td><code>senderKey</code>, <code>templateName</code>, <code>chatBubbleType</code>, <code>content</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>IMAGE</code></td>
<td>+ <code>imageUrl</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>WIDE</code></td>
<td>+ <code>imageUrl</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>WIDE_ITEM_LIST</code></td>
<td><code>senderKey</code>, <code>templateName</code>, <code>chatBubbleType</code>, <code>header</code>, <code>mainWideItem</code>, <code>subWideItemList</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>CAROUSEL_FEED</code></td>
<td><code>senderKey</code>, <code>templateName</code>, <code>chatBubbleType</code>, <code>carousel.list</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>PREMIUM_VIDEO</code></td>
<td><code>senderKey</code>, <code>templateName</code>, <code>chatBubbleType</code>, <code>video</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>COMMERCE</code></td>
<td>+ <code>imageUrl</code>, <code>commerce</code>, <code>buttons</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>CAROUSEL_COMMERCE</code></td>
<td><code>senderKey</code>, <code>templateName</code>, <code>chatBubbleType</code>, <code>carousel.list</code></td>
</tr>
</tbody>

<h2 id="템플릿-메시지-유형" data-spy-id="템플릿-메시지-유형" data-spy-section="가이드">템플릿 메시지 유형</h2>
<p><code>templateMessageType</code> 필드 값입니다.</p>
<div class="md-tablewrap"><table><thead>
<tr>
<th>코드</th>
<th>설명</th>
<th>비고</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>BA</code></td>
<td>기본형</td>
<td>—</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>EX</code></td>
<td>부가정보형</td>
<td><code>templateExtra</code> 필수</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>AD</code></td>
<td>채널추가형</td>
<td><code>buttons</code> 자동 삽입 (<code>AC</code>)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>MI</code></td>
<td>복합형</td>
<td><code>templateExtra</code> 필수, <code>buttons</code> 자동 삽입 (<code>AC</code>)</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></div><h2 id="템플릿-강조-유형" data-spy-id="템플릿-강조-유형" data-spy-section="가이드">템플릿 강조 유형</h2>
<p><code>templateEmphasizeType</code> 필드 값입니다.</p>
<div class="md-tablewrap"><table><thead>
<tr>
<th>코드</th>
<th>설명</th>
<th>필수 추가 필드</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>NONE</code></td>
<td>선택 안 함</td>
<td>—</td>

<td><code>templateTitle</code>, <code>templateSubtitle</code></td>
</tr>

<td><code>IMAGE</code></td>

</tr>

<td><code>templateItem.list</code></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></div><h2 id="발신-프로필-키-타입" data-spy-id="발신-프로필-키-타입" data-spy-section="가이드">발신 프로필 키 타입</h2>
<p><code>senderKeyType</code> 필드 값입니다.</p>
<ul>
<li><code>S</code> — 일반 발신프로필 (기본값)</li>
<li><code>G</code> — 발신프로필 그룹</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="템플릿-상태-변화" data-spy-id="템플릿-상태-변화" data-spy-section="가이드">템플릿 상태 변화</h2>
<ul>
<li><code>serviceStatus</code>: <code>REG</code> → <code>REQ</code> → <code>REJ</code> | <code>STP</code> | <code>RDY</code> → <code>ACT</code> → <code>DMT</code>/<code>BLK</code></li>
<li><code>status</code>: <code>S</code> (중지) / <code>A</code> (정상) / <code>R</code> (대기)</li>
<li><code>inspectionStatus</code>: <code>REG</code> → <code>REQ</code> → <code>REJ</code> | <code>APR</code> (승인)</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="버튼·바로연결-타입" data-spy-id="버튼·바로연결-타입" data-spy-section="가이드">버튼·바로연결 타입</h2>
